789993e owen.wen 2021-07-26

AOS-681: update DEMO keys

Symptom: device fused with DEMO key cannot boot
RootCause: CSR signed by CA server is not compatible with NXP boot ROM
Solution: Lewis create new SRK/IMG/CSF keys which has no "user defined extension" field

more information about the keys
https://atlassian.idtechproducts.com/confluence/display/EN/HAB%3A+import+new+keys+from+Lewis
https://atlassian.idtechproducts.com/confluence/display/EN/HAB+%28High+Assurance+Boot%29+and+fuse

Change-Id: Ibe15888659e35a4fea08db29f5cbe019afa28242
